Re: Personal network troubleshooting I’ve encountered similar cases where residents blame their ISP, but the real issue is outdated hardware or poor signal distribution. Consider placing your router centrally, away from microwaves or thick walls, and disabling guest networks if unused. Most consumer-grade routers degrade after three to four years. A new dual-band model under $100 often resolves these issues permanently.

Alternative solution for household connectivity issues Many clients report similar disruptions when their home Wi-Fi is managed by consumer-grade hardware. I’ve seen cases where a mesh system resolves intermittent drops, especially in multi-story homes. The problem isn’t usually the ISP—it’s signal fragmentation across rooms. A simple upgrade to dual-band routers with QoS settings often restores stability without additional fees.
